480 # A plugin that claims all the odd lines are executed, and none of 

481 # the even lines, and then punts reporting off to the built-in 

482 # Python reporting. 

483 import coverage.plugin 

484 class Plugin(coverage.CoveragePlugin): 

485 def file_tracer(self, filename): 

486 return OddTracer(filename) 

487 def file_reporter(self, filename): 

488 return "python" 

489 

490 class OddTracer(coverage.plugin.FileTracer): 

491 def __init__(self, filename): 

492 self.filename = filename 

493 def source_filename(self): 

494 return self.filename 

495 def line_number_range(self, frame): 

496 lineno = frame.f_lineno 

497 if lineno % 2: 

498 return (lineno, lineno) 

499 else: 

500 return (-1, -1) 

501 

502 def coverage_init(reg, options): 

503 reg.add_file_tracer(Plugin()) 

504 """)

532 import os 

533 import coverage.plugin 

534 class Plugin(coverage.CoveragePlugin): 

535 def file_tracer(self, filename): 

536 if filename.endswith("foo.py"): 

537 return MyTracer(filename) 

538 def file_reporter(self, filename): 

539 return MyReporter(filename) 

540 def find_executable_files(self, src_dir): 

541 # Check that src_dir is the right value 

542 files = os.listdir(src_dir) 

543 assert "foo.py" in files 

544 assert "unexecuted_plugin.py" in files 

545 return ["chimera.py"] 

546 

547 class MyTracer(coverage.plugin.FileTracer): 

548 def __init__(self, filename): 

549 self.filename = filename 

550 def source_filename(self): 

551 return self.filename 

552 def line_number_range(self, frame): 

553 return (999, 999) 

554 

555 class MyReporter(coverage.FileReporter): 

556 def lines(self): 

557 return {99, 999, 9999} 

558

560 reg.add_file_tracer(Plugin()) 

561 """)

727 import os.path 

728 import coverage.plugin 

729 class Plugin(coverage.plugin.CoveragePlugin): 

730 def __init__(self): 

731 self.calls = 0 

732 

733 def file_tracer(self, filename): 

734 print(filename) 

735 self.calls += 1 

736 if self.calls <= 2: 

737 return FileTracer(filename) 

738 else: 

739 17/0 # Oh noes! 

740 

741 class FileTracer(coverage.FileTracer): 

742 def __init__(self, filename): 

743 self.filename = filename 

744 def source_filename(self): 

745 return os.path.basename(self.filename).replace(".py", ".foo") 

746 def line_number_range(self, frame): 

747 return -1, -1 

748 

749 def coverage_init(reg, options):
